2025-06-01T01:52:20.8072986Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8073335Z         You can read more about "package discovery" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8073346Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8073698Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/package_discovery.html
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8073710Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8074044Z         If you don't want 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' to be distributed and are
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8074376Z         already explicitly excluding 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' via
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8074706Z         `find_namespace_packages(...)/find_namespace` or `find_packages(...)/find`,
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8075042Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8075362Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8075387Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8075726Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8075737Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8076033Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8076042Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8076048Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8076495Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8076693Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8077136Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8077367Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8077521Z         ********************************************************************************
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8077531Z 
2025-06-01T01:52:20.8077637Z !!
